\"github.com/sg-evals/llvm-project--a8f3c97d\", \"path\": \"llvm/lib/CodeGen/StackProtector.cpp\", \"symbol\": \"InsertStackProtectors\"},\n    {\"repo\": \"github.com/sg-evals/llvm-project--a8f3c97d\", \"path\": \"llvm/lib/CodeGen/StackProtector.cpp\", \"symbol\": \"CreateFailBB\"},\n    {\"repo\": \"github.com/sg-evals/llvm-project--a8f3c97d\", \"path\": \"llvm/lib/CodeGen/SafeStack.cpp\", \"symbol\": \"SafeStack\"},\n    {\"repo\": \"github.com/sg-evals/llvm-project--a8f3c97d\", \"path\": \"libc/src/compiler/generic/__stack_chk_fail.cpp\", \"symbol\": \"__stack_chk_fail\"}\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"Stack protection mechanisms against buffer overflow attacks in LLVM are implemented across multiple layers:\\n\\n1. **StackProtector Pass (llvm/lib/CodeGen/StackProtector.cpp, llvm/include/llvm/CodeGen/StackProtector.h)**: The primary LLVM pass that inserts stack protector checks into functions. The StackProtector class is a FunctionPass that implements the stack smashing protection mechanism by loading a guard value before local variable allocations and checking it after (on function exit). Key functions include InsertStackProtectors() which inserts the prologue and epilogue code, CreateFailBB() which creates the failure path when the guard is corrupted, and SSPLayoutAnalysis which determines which functions require protection.\\n\\n2. **SafeStack Pass (llvm/lib/CodeGen/SafeStack.cpp, llvm/include/llvm/CodeGen/SafeStack.h)**: Implements the SafeStack instrumentation pass that separates the stack into safe and unsafe portions. The SafeStack class (llvm/lib/CodeGen/SafeStack.cpp) performs the actual IR transformation, while SafeStackPass and SafeStackLegacyPass provide the pass interfaces. This mechanism protects against stack-based attacks by placing dangerous allocations (arrays, structures containing arrays) onto an explicitly managed unsafe stack.\\n\\n3. **SafeStackLayout (llvm/lib/CodeGen/SafeStackLayout.cpp, llvm/lib/CodeGen/SafeStackLayout.h)**: Manages the frame layout for the unsafe stack used by SafeStack, determining how allocations are arranged in memory.\\n\\n4. **SafeStack Runtime (compiler-rt/lib/safestack/safestack.cpp)**: Provides runtime support for SafeStack, including allocation and deallocation of unsafe stack memory for threads.\\n\\n5. **Stack Protector Runtime (__stack_chk_fail implementation): Located in libc/src/compiler/generic/__stack_chk_fail.cpp, this provides the actual __stack_chk_fail() function called when stack corruption is detected. It prints \\\"stack smashing detected\\\" and aborts execution. The __stack_chk_guard variable (also in this file) contains the guard value used to detect corruption.
